msg:Environment: The environment is very good. It is on the 18th floor. I stayed in room 1807. It has a 180-degree view and three floor-to-ceiling windows, which feels very bright.
Hygiene: The bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, and there is a large bathtub. The waiter cleans it promptly and cleanly every day. There are many choices of sheets, quilts and pillows, which are very comfortable. The mattress is moderately soft and hard, and it is good for rest.
Facilities: Sofas, recliners, and desks are available to meet various needs, such as playing cards, working, and leisure. There is a swimming pool on the fourth floor, and I swam there once.
Service: The breakfast buffet has a rich variety, and the time is until 11 o'clock. Various meals are replenished in time. There are good night porridge, small gifts, and milk for free, which is very considerate.

name:Bâ€aâ€oâ€xâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€g
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted February 27, 2024
msg:I was not satisfied with the king-size bed room I booked on the first night because the wash basin in the bathroom shower was exposed and very noisy, and it was even noisier because it was close to the road. Of course, this is a design problem of the hotel. The twin room I changed to the next day was much better and quieter, with real dry and wet separation.
Service: The service of the front desk and the aunt was very good, and they were more patient to answer customers' questions. The cleaning aunt sent desserts for two consecutive nights and wrote a small note, which was very heartwarming. The only thing is that the hotel shows that it is a five-star hotel, but it is not up to the five-star standard. The details are reflected, there is no aromatherapy, conditioner, body lotion, etc. Overall, I am satisfied!
Location: Although it is in Yuelu District, a little far from the city center, there is a subway station at the entrance of the hotel, and the transportation is very convenient, but there are more standings.
Meals: Although there are not many types of buffets, there are basically Chinese and Western meals. Milk and soy milk are delicious, and the soup noodles are a bit lumpy. Everything else is ok, and the food is relatively fresh.
Parking: The underground garage of the hotel is the parking lot, with many spaces, free, and no need to drive when traveling.
Hygiene: I am satisfied with the hygiene, at least I can't see any dirt with the naked eye.

msg:During the Chinese New Year, I came to Changsha. This hotel is very cost-effective. After all, the environment and facilities in the hotel are very good. I saw others say that Yannian is a local hotel brand in Changsha. There are many stores in Changsha. This one is cheaper because of its geographical location. The advantage is that there is a subway station downstairs, so you can hang out until late and come back. The disadvantage is that there is nothing to visit around the hotel, no shops or businesses. It is just right to come back and sleep after eating and drinking enough. However, the hotel is really high-end and has a four-star rating. When we checked in, I asked for a quiet room, so the staff arranged it for me on the 25th floor. The room window faces the road, but there is no outside during the Chinese New Year. I stayed for one night, but I thought the hotel was so good, so I extended it for another night. The bug on the second night was that the floor was too high, and there was a strong wind at night, which was noisy. The hotel has self-service laundry on the 12th floor, which is good and suitable for people like us who have been out for a long time. The hotel breakfast is relatively rich. The disadvantage is that there are too many people, the table is not cleared in time, and the dishes are piled on the table. People have no place to sit with plates, so I didnâ€™t go to eat breakfast the next day, but I swiped my card and packed a portion for the children to eat on the way. This hotel room is really good, and parking is also very convenient, with no limit on the number of times. Tell the front desk before going out. I think the ground parking space is more convenient. The mattress is very comfortable, the bedding is very clean, and the service attitude of the front desk staff is very goodğŸ‘
